info:Stayed in May 2024

info:1 Review
rating:4.5
posted:Posted May 4, 2024
msg:I didn't take photos. I booked a 0-pressure family room. The mattress rebounded slowly and the bedding was clean and tidy. The fried rice for breakfast was very good. The room was also equipped with laundry detergent, which was thoughtful.

The plan was to check in after climbing Tianzhu Mountain. There were few local chain hotels to choose from, so I chose the one that looked the most impressive.

The surprise was that the service was very good. After opening the car door, someone took the initiative to help me carry the suitcase to the door. The front desk was also very professional and the check-in was fast and smooth.

Like the innovation of the thank you coin. You can reward the service staff with an equivalent of 10 yuan, or you can transfer it to cash. When we left, we left it to the uncle carrying the suitcase. I look forward to the hotel service getting better and better. I will stay again next time.
